<Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
Well-executed and made with care. I personally have a thing for paper thin red onions - and these are dressed in lime juice. A perfect counter point to the lamb and beans. Mistura's rotisserie chicken is also a solid choice. Loved the plantains. Next, I want to try one of the empanadas,  or the chicken in walnut curry sauce, or their lomo saltado a beef dish. Irene is welcoming, warm and genuine. For reasonably priced, well-made food check Mistura out.</Review>

< text>
Nice cafe with a view, indoor and outdoor door seating, plenty of wait staff and free refill for tea! Good range of salads, sandwiches, hour and cold drinks. And if you want just a hard boiled egg, you can find it here too. Sure the prices are steep here, but which museum with captive audience don't do that? So if you want to economise, being a packed lunch to have on the beautiful lawns and seats then come in here for refillable teas.<//text>

<Date>1525395476055< /Date>< review>
First a warning to visitors who don‚Äôt know the de Young Cafe system: in addition to their pricey menu you will be charged a surcharge which is a percentage to pay for their health insurance. Foreign visitors of course will also be surprised by the additional sales tax. I asked the cashier girl why the tax was so high and she still would not disclose the health insurance surcharge until I read my receipt - not very professional. It felt like she had intentions to deceive the customer.
In terms of their food: it is just so so. I had a pre-made turkey sandwich. The french bread they used was tough at the least. Instead of lettuce they used shredded cabbage. I suppose it prevents the sandwich from getting soggy. I didn‚Äôt have the chance to try anything else because they were getting ready to close.
Service was average. Most workers were not that into the job.< /review>

<text>Ahhhhhh, I love this place. üòÄ

Words. Words. Words. Visions. Dreams. New worlds of challenging and exciting explorations.

If you want to explore some magic in amazing Northern California - The Magic starts here, right in little old Willits. Small town, big heart and endless magic when you remember to slow down and embrace being in a slow moving, blessed miracle community. The future!

The Book Juggler is like stepping into a powerful magical realm of universal imaginations - where we mere humans think we are wisely choosing books, but the books have chosen us. üìö Like a wand choosing a Wizard.

This has only happened one other time in my life in a four hundred year old bookstore in Norway, where the books found me. Now in your enchanted distribution hall of dreams it happens again. Thank you.

Northern California is soooooo fortunate to have a powerful magical portal to explore the true joyful spirit of reading and remember the truth of words that create our imaginations of the future.

I am so grateful that my wise elders were present enough to drag me constantly into all places that honored books. So I too, would always continue my love affair with those that so generously and painstakingly pressed their thoughts onto paper for all of us to share in their quest for a truly more magical and better world for all of us.

The Book Juggler, where books choose you.

This is regarding the Goleta, California Public Storage site, location #75078.

My experience, from start to finish, was five-star!

The customer service gentleman, who answered my first call to inquire about renting a storage unit, was super patient with all of my questions. He was knowledgeable about every aspect of renting the unit.

Kristina, the manager of the site, was very thorough explaining the process of renting the unit, accessing the unit, and the future process to exit (close out) the unit. Thank you staff!

I highly recommend storing your belongings here.<//review>

<review>Originally planned on having them clean just my upstairs carpet and stairs.  They were having a 50% off sale on tile cleaning so I had them do my downstairs tile as well.  The carpets came out great and I paid the extra $30 for them to use the big machine which pulled a bad stain out.  Price for carpet was great, $155 + $30 for big machine to do the entire upstairs, 3 bedrooms, halls, stairs, and closets.  Tile cleaning is pricey, $1 per sq ft without sale, $0.50 with sale.  I also had them clean one cushion on my light colored couch because one of our cats got sick on it and even though we cleaned it up, still had a faint spot.  $25 to clean the cushion and it looks like brand new again.  The reason I'm not giving 5 stars is because the tile was still dirty in the corners so I had to do some touch up work myself.  The machine they use is round so it doesn't get the corners well.  Also, I had to touch up some places on the tile where it looked like there was solution dried and several foot prints in the solution.  Basically when the light hits it you could see spots.  I just had to touch it up with a wet rag, but for $240 tile price ($450 total job) I felt like I shouldn't have to do any touch up work.  These are of course things you don't notice until later when you think it should be dry but the spots don't go away.  Overall I'm happy with my much cleaner home and would call them again in the future if I wasn't planning to replace my carpet with wood flooring.< /review>< Rating>
